ACTOR Abaddon 
{
Health 650
Speed 8
FloatSpeed 5

Height 56

+MISSILEMORE
States
{
Spawn:
         ABDD A 1 A_Look
		 Loop
See:
         ABDD A 3 A_Chase
		 TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(13,"Evade")		 
         Loop
Evade:
		 TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,7)
		 TNT1 A 0 ThrustThing(Angle*256/360+64,14,0,0)
		 ABDD AAAA 3 A_Chase
		 TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
		 Goto See
		 TNT1 A 0 ThrustThing(Angle*256/360+192,14,0,0)		 
		 ABDD AAAA 3 A_Chase
		 TNT1 A 0 A_Stop		 
		 Goto See
Missile:
         TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"Seeking")
Normal:
         ABDD BC 6 A_FaceTarget
         ABDD D 2 Bright A_FaceTarget
		 ABDD D 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("ABDBall",24,0,0,0,0)
         TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("ABDBall",24,0,6,0,0)
         ABDD D 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("ABDBall",24,0,-6,0,0)
		 ABDD CB 4 A_FaceTarget
		 ABDD D 2 Bright A_FaceTarget
		 ABDD D 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("ABDBall",24,0,0,0,0)
         TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("ABDBall",24,0,6,0,0)
         ABDD D 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("ABDBall",24,0,-6,0,0)
         ABDD CB 4 A_FaceTarget
	     TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(87,"Seeking")
         Goto See
Seeking:
         ABDD BC 6 A_Facetarget
	     ABDD D 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("HeleBall",24,0,0,0,0)
         ABDD CB 4	
	    Goto See
Melee:
         ABDD BC 5 A_FaceTarget
         ABDD D 5 A_MeleeAttack
		 ABDD CB 5 A_FaceTarget
         Goto See
Pain:
		 ABDD E 3
		 ABDD F 6 A_Pain
         Goto See
Death:
         ABDD G 8 A_Scream
         ABDD H 8 A_NoBlocking
		 ABDD H -1
		 Stop
Crash:
		 TNT1 A 0
		 TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
		 ABDD I 4 A_PlaySound("Gore/Splat")
		 ABDD J 4 A_NoBlocking
		 ABDD K 4
		 ABDD L -1 A_SetFloorClip
		 Stop
Raise:
	     TNT1 A 0
	     TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("VileHealEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
	     ABDD KJIHG 4
	     Goto See         
         }
}

}Actor Agaures : Imp 21718
{
  Obituary "%o fell before an agaures."
  HitObituary "%o was cut open by an agaures."
  Health 140
  Radius 20
  Height 56
  Mass 500
  Speed 10
  PainChance 80
  MeleeDamage 4
  DropItem "LifeEssence" 100
  DropItem "ArmorBonusMax" 100
  DropItem "DemonAmmo" 100
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +QUICKTORETALIATE
  +MissileMore
  SeeSound "superimp/sight"
  PainSound "voidimp/pain"
  DeathSound "superimp/death"
  ActiveSound "superimp/active"
  MeleeSound "imps/melee"
  MONSTER
  +FLOORCLIP
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    AGUR A 10 A_Look
    loop
  See:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(46,"Evade")
   	AGUR AABB 3 A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("HumanishStep",0,0,0,0)
	AGUR CCDD 3 A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("HumanishStep",0,0,0,0)
    loop
  Evade:
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,7)
	TNT1 A 0 ThrustThing(Angle*256/360+64,16,0,0)
	AGUR AAAA 3 A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
	Goto See
	TNT1 A 0 ThrustThing(Angle*256/360+192,16,0,0)
	AGUR AAAA 3 A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
	Goto See
  Melee:
    AGUR W 5 A_FaceTarget
    AGUR X 1 A_PlaySound("agaures/swing")
    AGUR X 5 A_FaceTarget
    AGUR Y 3 A_MeleeAttack
    goto See
  Missile:
	AGUR A 0 A_Jump(100,"Burst")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250,"Lunge")
    AGUR EF 5 A_FaceTarget
    AGUR G 0 A_CustomMissile("AgauresBall", 37, 0, 7, 0, 0)
    AGUR G 0 A_CustomMissile("AgauresBall", 37, 0, -7, 0, 0)
    AGUR G 3 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("AgauresBall", 37, 0, 0, 0, 0)
    goto See
  Burst:
    AGUR EF 5 A_FaceTarget
	AGUR G 0 A_CustomMissile("SpeedyAgauresBall", 37, 0, -10, 0, 0)
	AGUR G 0 A_CustomMissile("SpeedyAgauresBall", 37, 0, 0, 0, 0)
    AGUR G 3 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("SpeedyAgauresBall", 37, 0, 10, 0, 0)
	AGUR EF 5 A_FaceTarget
	AGUR G 0 A_CustomMissile("SpeedyAgauresBall", 37, 0, -10, 0, 0)
	AGUR G 0 A_CustomMissile("SpeedyAgauresBall", 37, 0, 0, 0, 0)
    AGUR G 3 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("SpeedyAgauresBall",37,0,10,0,0)
	AGUR EF 5 A_FaceTarget
	goto see
Lunge:
	   TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(200,1)
	   Goto See
	   TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("agaures/swing")
	   AGUR WW 5 A_FaceTarget
	   TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(SLIDESONWALLS,1)
	   TNT1 A 0 ThrustThingZ(0,20,0,1)
	   AGUR X 2 A_Recoil(-24)
	   AGUR X 3 A_CustomMissile("ImpLunge",18,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	   AGUR Y 6
	   AGUR Y 2 A_ScaleVelocity(0.2)
	   TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(SLIDESONWALLS,0)
	   AGUR Y 1 A_ScaleVelocity(0)
	   Goto See
  Pain:
    TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(SLIDESONWALLS,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(87,"PainMissile")
    AGUR H 2
    AGUR H 2 A_Pain
    goto See
  PainMissile:
    TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(SLIDESONWALLS,0)
    AGUR H 2
    AGUR H 2 A_Pain
    goto See
  Death:
    TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(SLIDESONWALLS,0)
    AGUR I 8
    AGUR J 8 A_Scream
    AGUR KL 6 A_SpawnItem("BodyCrash",0,0,0,0)
    AGUR M 6 A_NoBlocking
    AGUR N -1
    stop
  XDeath:
    TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(SLIDESONWALLS,0)
    AGUR O 5
    AGUR P 5 A_XScream
    AGUR Q 5 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
    AGUR R 5 A_NoBlocking
    AGUR STU 5
    AGUR V -1
    stop
  Raise:
   	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("VileHealEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    AGUR MLKJI 5
    goto See
  }
}

  DropItem "ArmorPlate" 120

  DropItem "MineAmmo" 100 1

  +MissileMore

  {

    ZBMB AB 10 A_Look
    Loop

    ZBMB A 0 A_PlaySound("suicide/loop")
    Loop

    ZBMB A 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("suicide/run")
    ZBMB AAAA 5 A_FaceTarget
	ZBMB A 1 A_Jump(256,2)
	ZBMB A 0 A_JumpIf(velx != 0 || vely != 0,1)
	Goto ChargeStop

	ZBMB A 0 A_GiveInventory("SuicideJumping",1)
    ZBMB A 0 A_Recoil(-11)
    ZBMB ABCD 1 A_JumpIfCloser(90,"Melee")
	ZBMB A 0 A_FaceTarget
	ZBMB A 0 A_Recoil(-11)
    ZBMB ABCD 1 A_JumpIfCloser(90,"Melee")
	ZBMB A 0 A_FaceTarget
	ZBMB A 0 A_Recoil(-11)
    ZBMB ABCD 1 A_JumpIfCloser(90,"Melee")
	ZBMB A 0 A_FaceTarget
	ZBMB A 0 A_Recoil(-11)
	ZBMB A 0 A_JumpIf(z - floorz >= 64,"ChargeStop")
    ZBMB ABCD 1 A_JumpIfCloser(90,"Melee")
    Goto Missile+6
  ChargeStop:
    ZBMB A 1 A_Stop
    Goto See		
  Melee:
    ZBMB A 2 A_Die
    Stop
  Pain:
    ZBMB A 3
    ZBMB A 3 A_Pain
    Goto See
  Death:
    TNT1 A 0
    TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("SuicideBomb",24,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("OrangeParticleSpawner",0,0,24,0,0,0,0,128) 
    TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom3",24,0,random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX2",24,0,random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
    TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Debris",0,0,24,Random(4,-4),Random(4,-4),Random(4,8),0,128)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("RocketEx",0,24)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
    ZBMB M 5 Bright A_PlaySound("weapons/rocklx")
    ZBMB N 5 Bright A_XScream

    ZBMB U -1
    Stop

        TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("phaseimp/teleport")
		PELE E 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.15)
        PELE E 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.35)
        PELE E 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.55)

		PELE ED 4
		Goto See
	Seeker:

		PELE E 4 Bright	A_FaceTarget

		PELE F 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PhaseEleBall", 26, 0, -30)
		PELE F 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("PhaseEleBall", 26, 0, 30)
		PELE ED 4
		Goto See
	Melee:
	    TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1)
        PELE DE 5 A_FaceTarget 
        PELE F 4 A_MeleeAttack
	    PELE ED 3 A_FaceTarget
        Goto See		
	Pain:
	    TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(61,"PainMissile")
		PELE G 12 A_Pain
		Goto See
	PainMissile:
	    TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1)
		PELE G 12 A_Pain
		Goto Missile	
	Death:
	    TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1)
		PELE H 5 
		PELE I 5 Bright A_Scream
		PELE J 5 Bright A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.75,1)

	    TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PurpleParticleSpawner", 0, 0, random(20,40), 0, 0, 0, 0, 128)

		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom8", random(20,40), 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))		
		PELE K 5 Bright A_PainDie("PhaseSoul")
		PELE LM 5 Bright
		Stop
      }

    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Pause","SeekMissile","SeekMissile2")
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpidRefire
	Goto AutoCannon+2
  SeekMissile:
    WDMK EEEE 3 A_FaceTarget
	WDMK F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("HellFireRocket",40,0,0)
	WDMK E 3 A_FaceTarget
	WDMK F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("HellFireRocket",40,0,0)
	WDMK E 3 Bright
	Goto see
  SeekMissile2:
    WDMK G 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz-floorz<=175,"SeekMissile")
    WDMK G 1 A_FaceTarget
	WDMK G 5 
	WDMK G 1 A_FaceTarget
	WDMK G 3 A_PlaySound("widowmaker/beep")
	WDMK G 1 A_FaceTarget
	WDMK G 3 A_PlaySound("widowmaker/beep")
	WDMK G 1 A_FaceTarget
	WDMK G 3 A_PlaySound("widowmaker/beep")
	WDMK G 1 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("widowmaker/launch")
    WDMK H 4 Bright
	WDMK H 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("widowmakerMiniRockets",55,40,-25,90) 
	WDMK H 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("widowmakerMiniRockets",55,25,0,90) 
	WDMK H 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("widowmakerMiniRockets",55,10,25,90) 
    WDMK H 2 Bright A_FaceTarget
	WDMK G 2
    Goto See
  Pain:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(80,"PainMissile")
    WDMK I 5
    WDMK I 5 A_Pain
    Goto See
   PainMissile:
    WDMK I 5
    WDMK I 5 A_Pain
    Goto Missile
  XDeath:
  Death:
    WDMK I 7 A_Scream 
	WDMK I 2 Bright 
	TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX2", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))	
	WDMK IIJJJ 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("Kaboom17", Random(10,50), 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX2", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))	
	WDMK JJJKK 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("Kaboom17", Random(10,50), 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX2", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))	
	WDMK KKLLL 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("Kaboom17", Random(10,50), 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX2", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
    WDMK M 6 A_NoBlocking
    WDMK N -1
    Stop
  Raise:
    TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("VileHealEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    WDMK N -1
    Stop
	}   
}
